     <p>Among the individuals who have attended or graduated from the University of Virginia are author <a href="/wiki/Edgar_Allan_Poe" title="Edgar Allan Poe">Edgar Allan Poe</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-da-poe_144-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-da-poe-144"><span>[</span>144<span>]</span></a></sup> medical researcher <a href="/wiki/Walter_Reed" title="Walter Reed">Walter Reed</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-da-reed_145-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-da-reed-145"><span>[</span>145<span>]</span></a></sup> painter <a href="/wiki/Georgia_O%27Keeffe" title="Georgia O'Keeffe">Georgia O'Keeffe</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-da-okeeffe_146-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-da-okeeffe-146"><span>[</span>146<span>]</span></a></sup> polar explorer <a href="/wiki/Richard_Evelyn_Byrd" title="Richard Evelyn Byrd" class="mw-redirect">Richard Byrd</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-da-byrd_147-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-da-byrd-147"><span>[</span>147<span>]</span></a></sup> computer scientist <a href="/wiki/John_Backus" title="John Backus">John Backus</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-da-backus_148-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-da-backus-148"><span>[</span>148<span>]</span></a></sup> pioneer kidney transplant surgeon <a href="/wiki/J._Hartwell_Harrison" title="J. Hartwell Harrison">J. Hartwell Harrison</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149"><span>[</span>149<span>]</span></a></sup> five <a href="/wiki/NASA" title="NASA">NASA</a> astronauts (<a href="/wiki/Patrick_G._Forrester" title="Patrick G. Forrester">Patrick G. Forrester</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-forrester_150-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-forrester-150"><span>[</span>150<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Karl_Gordon_Henize" title="Karl Gordon Henize">Karl Gordon Henize</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-henize_151-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-henize-151"><span>[</span>151<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Bill_Nelson" title="Bill Nelson">Bill Nelson</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-whorunsgov_152-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-whorunsgov-152"><span>[</span>152<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Marshburn" title="Thomas Marshburn">Thomas Marshburn</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-marshburn_153-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-marshburn-153"><span>[</span>153<span>]</span></a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Kathryn_C._Thornton" title="Kathryn C. Thornton">Kathryn C. Thornton</a>),<sup id="cite_ref-na-thornton-k_154-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-thornton-k-154"><span>[</span>154<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Deep_sea_vent" title="Deep sea vent" class="mw-redirect">deep sea vent</a> researcher <a href="/wiki/Richard_Lutz" title="Richard Lutz" class="mw-redirect">Richard Lutz</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-proffesor_155-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-proffesor-155"><span>[</span>155<span>]</span></a></sup> NASA Launch Director <a href="/wiki/Michael_D._Leinbach" title="Michael D. Leinbach">Michael D. Leinbach</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-va_156-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-va-156"><span>[</span>156<span>]</span></a></sup> Pulitzer Prize-winning poets <a href="/wiki/Karl_Shapiro" title="Karl Shapiro">Karl Shapiro</a><sup id="cite_ref-na-va_156-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-va-156"><span>[</span>156<span>]</span></a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Henry_S._Taylor" title="Henry S. Taylor">Henry S. Taylor</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-va_156-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-va-156"><span>[</span>156<span>]</span></a></sup> short story writer <a href="/wiki/Breece_D%27J_Pancake" title="Breece D'J Pancake">Breece D'J Pancake</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-pancake_157-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-pancake-157"><span>[</span>157<span>]</span></a></sup> Director of the <a href="/wiki/National_Institutes_of_Health" title="National Institutes of Health">National Institutes of Health</a> <a href="/wiki/Francis_Collins_(geneticist)" title="Francis Collins (geneticist)" class="mw-redirect">Francis Collins</a>, <a href="/w/index.php?title=Dale_Elizabeth_Wright&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Dale Elizabeth Wright (page does not exist)">Dale Elizabeth Wright</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-va_156-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-va-156"><span>[</span>156<span>]</span></a></sup> journalist <a href="/wiki/Katie_Couric" title="Katie Couric">Katie Couric</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-va_156-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-va-156"><span>[</span>156<span>]</span></a></sup> journalist <a href="/wiki/Margaret_Brennan" title="Margaret Brennan">Margaret Brennan</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-va_156-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-va-156"><span>[</span>156<span>]</span></a></sup> author <a href="/wiki/David_Nolan_(American_author)" title="David Nolan (American author)">David Nolan</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-nolan_158-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-nolan-158"><span>[</span>158<span>]</span></a></sup> comedian and creator of <a href="/wiki/30_Rock" title="30 Rock">30 Rock</a> <a href="/wiki/Tina_Fey" title="Tina Fey">Tina Fey</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-va_156-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-va-156"><span>[</span>156<span>]</span></a></sup> film director <a href="/wiki/Tom_Shadyac" title="Tom Shadyac">Tom Shadyac</a>, author <a href="/wiki/Barbara_A._Perry" title="Barbara A. Perry">Barbara A. Perry</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-perry_159-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-perry-159"><span>[</span>159<span>]</span></a></sup> musician <a href="/wiki/Boyd_Tinsley" title="Boyd Tinsley">Boyd Tinsley</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-boyd_160-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-boyd-160"><span>[</span>160<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Jens_S%C3%B6ring" title="Jens S&ouml;ring">Jens S&ouml;ring</a>, <a href="/wiki/Elizabeth_Haysom" title="Elizabeth Haysom">Elizabeth Haysom</a>, <a href="/wiki/Billionaire" title="Billionaire">billionaire</a> commodity trader <a href="/wiki/Paul_Tudor_Jones" title="Paul Tudor Jones">Paul Tudor Jones</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-va_156-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-va-156"><span>[</span>156<span>]</span></a></sup> noted philanthropist and founder of <a href="/wiki/Landmark_Media_Enterprises" title="Landmark Media Enterprises">Landmark Communications</a> <a href="/wiki/Frank_Batten" title="Frank Batten">Frank Batten</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-va_156-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-va-156"><span>[</span>156<span>]</span></a></sup> influential <a href="/wiki/Indie_rock" title="Indie rock">indie rock</a> artist <a href="/wiki/Stephen_Malkmus" title="Stephen Malkmus">Stephen Malkmus</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-va_156-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-va-156"><span>[</span>156<span>]</span></a></sup> hip-hop artist and <a href="/wiki/Peabody_Award" title="Peabody Award">Peabody Award</a> winner <a href="/wiki/Asheru" title="Asheru">Asheru</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-asheru_161-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-asheru-161"><span>[</span>161<span>]</span></a></sup> TV personality <a href="/wiki/Vern_Yip" title="Vern Yip">Vern Yip</a> <sup id="cite_ref-na-yip_162-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-yip-162"><span>[</span>162<span>]</span></a></sup> and TV political commentator <a href="/wiki/Michael_Shure" title="Michael Shure">Michael Shure</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-163" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-163"><span>[</span>163<span>]</span></a></sup></p> 
     <p>Notable athletes who have attended or graduated from the University of Virginia include 3-time <a href="/wiki/Naismith_College_Player_of_the_Year" title="Naismith College Player of the Year">NCAA Player of the Year</a> for men's basketball <a href="/wiki/Ralph_Sampson" title="Ralph Sampson">Ralph Sampson</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-va_156-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-va-156"><span>[</span>156<span>]</span></a></sup> pro wrestler <a href="/wiki/Mike_Jones_(wrestler)" title="Mike Jones (wrestler)">Virgil</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-virgil_164-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-virgil-164"><span>[</span>164<span>]</span></a></sup> 3-time Olympic Gold Medalist for women's basketball <a href="/wiki/Dawn_Staley" title="Dawn Staley">Dawn Staley</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-va_156-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-va-156"><span>[</span>156<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/New_England_Patriots" title="New England Patriots">New England Patriots</a> Long Snapper <a href="/wiki/Danny_Aiken" title="Danny Aiken">Danny Aiken</a>, NFL Pro Bowlers <a href="/wiki/Ronde_Barber" title="Ronde Barber">Ronde Barber</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-va_156-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-va-156"><span>[</span>156<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Tiki_Barber" title="Tiki Barber">Tiki Barber</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-va_156-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-va-156"><span>[</span>156<span>]</span></a></sup> and James Farrior;<sup id="cite_ref-165" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-165"><span>[</span>165<span>]</span></a></sup> NFL Super Bowl appearances <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Jones_(American_football)" title="Thomas Jones (American football)">Thomas Jones</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-thomasjones_166-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-thomasjones-166"><span>[</span>166<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Antwan_Harris" title="Antwan Harris">Antwan Harris</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-harris_167-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-harris-167"><span>[</span>167<span>]</span></a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Terrence_Wilkins" title="Terrence Wilkins">Terrence Wilkins</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-wilkins_168-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-wilkins-168"><span>[</span>168<span>]</span></a></sup> and professional baseball players <a href="/wiki/Mark_Reynolds_(baseball)" title="Mark Reynolds (baseball)">Mark Reynolds</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ryan_Zimmerman" title="Ryan Zimmerman">Ryan Zimmerman</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-va_156-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-va-156"><span>[</span>156<span>]</span></a></sup> Olympic medalist <a href="/wiki/Wyatt_Allen" title="Wyatt Allen">Wyatt Allen</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-va_156-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-va-156"><span>[</span>156<span>]</span></a></sup> Indian tennis player <a href="/wiki/Somdev_Devvarman" title="Somdev Devvarman">Somdev Devvarman</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-devvarman_169-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-devvarman-169"><span>[</span>169<span>]</span></a></sup> The University of Virginia has been home to several top soccer players throughout the years ? several former U.Va. players have gone on to play for the <a href="/wiki/United_States_men%27s_national_soccer_team" title="United States men's national soccer team">United States men's national soccer team</a>, including <a href="/wiki/Tony_Meola" title="Tony Meola">Tony Meola</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-meola_170-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-meola-170"><span>[</span>170<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Jeff_Agoos" title="Jeff Agoos">Jeff Agoos</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-agoos_171-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-agoos-171"><span>[</span>171<span>]</span></a></sup> and former USA team captains <a href="/wiki/Claudio_Reyna" title="Claudio Reyna">Claudio Reyna</a><sup id="cite_ref-na-reyna_172-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-reyna-172"><span>[</span>172<span>]</span></a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/John_Harkes" title="John Harkes">John Harkes</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-na-harkes_173-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-harkes-173"><span>[</span>173<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Nikki_Krzysik" title="Nikki Krzysik">Nikki Krzysik</a> went on to play soccer professionally in the <a href="/wiki/Women%27s_Professional_Soccer" title="Women's Professional Soccer">WPS</a> and <a href="/wiki/National_Women%27s_Soccer_League" title="National Women's Soccer League">NWSL</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-174" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-174"><span>[</span>174<span>]</span></a></sup></p> 
     <p>Numerous political leaders have also attended the University of Virginia, including the 28th President of the United States, <a href="/wiki/Woodrow_Wilson" title="Woodrow Wilson">Woodrow Wilson</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-da-wilson_175-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-da-wilson-175"><span>[</span>175<span>]</span></a></sup> the 18th Speaker of the United States House of Representatives <a href="/wiki/Robert_Mercer_Taliaferro_Hunter" title="Robert Mercer Taliaferro Hunter" class="mw-redirect">Robert Mercer Taliaferro Hunter</a>, U.S. Senator and 1968 Presidential candidate <a href="/wiki/Robert_F._Kennedy" title="Robert F. Kennedy">Robert F. Kennedy</a><sup id="cite_ref-na-va_156-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-va-156"><span>[</span>156<span>]</span></a></sup> (Law School), and his brother, Senator <a href="/wiki/Ted_Kennedy" title="Ted Kennedy">Ted Kennedy</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-va_156-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-va-156"><span>[</span>156<span>]</span></a></sup> New York House of Representative candidate <a href="/wiki/Sean_Patrick_Maloney" title="Sean Patrick Maloney">Sean Patrick Maloney</a>.,<sup id="cite_ref-Class_of_1988_176-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Class_of_1988-176"><span>[</span>176<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Attorney_General_of_Virginia" title="Attorney General of Virginia">Attorney General of Virginia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ken_Cuccinelli" title="Ken Cuccinelli">Ken Cuccinelli</a> (<a href="/wiki/University_of_Virginia_School_of_Engineering_and_Applied_Science" title="University of Virginia School of Engineering and Applied Science">SEAS</a>), and <a href="/wiki/Janet_Napolitano" title="Janet Napolitano">Janet Napolitano</a> (<a href="/wiki/University_of_Virginia_School_of_Law" title="University of Virginia School of Law">Law</a>).</p> 
     <p>Many of Virginia's governors studied at the University, including <a href="/wiki/Colgate_Darden" title="Colgate Darden">Colgate Darden</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-darden_177-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-darden-177"><span>[</span>177<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/George_Allen_(U.S._politician)" title="George Allen (U.S. politician)">George Allen</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-na-va_156-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-va-156"><span>[</span>156<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Albertis_S._Harrison,_Jr." title="Albertis S. Harrison, Jr.">Albertis S. Harrison, Jr.</a>, <a href="/wiki/Frederick_W._M._Holliday" title="Frederick W. M. Holliday">Frederick W. M. Holliday</a>, <a href="/wiki/Claude_A._Swanson" title="Claude A. Swanson">Claude A. Swanson</a>, <a href="/wiki/Elbert_Lee_Trinkle" title="Elbert Lee Trinkle">Elbert Lee Trinkle</a>, <a href="/wiki/John_S._Battle" title="John S. Battle">John S. Battle</a>, <a href="/wiki/James_Lindsay_Almond,_Jr." title="James Lindsay Almond, Jr.">James Lindsay Almond, Jr.</a>, <a href="/wiki/John_N._Dalton" title="John N. Dalton">John N. Dalton</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gerald_L._Baliles" title="Gerald L. Baliles">Gerald L. Baliles</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Jim_Gilmore" title="Jim Gilmore">Jim Gilmore</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-na-va_156-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-na-va-156"><span>[</span>156<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
